function gBits32() local a,b,c,d=Byte(ByteString,DIP,DIP + 3 );DIP=DIP + 4 ;return (d * 16777216) + (c * 65536) + (b * 256) + a ;end local function gFloat() local Left=gBits32();local (Mantissa==0) then return Sign * 0 ;else Exponent=1;IsNormal=0;end elseif (Exponent==2047) then return ((Mantissa==0) and (Sign * (1/0))) or (Sign * NaN) ;end return LDExp(Sign,Exponent-1023 ) *
